issued a press release announcing its unaudited financial results for the quarter ended March 31, 2023. A copy of the press release making
the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>IT Tech Packaging,
Inc. Announces First Quarter 2023 Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;May
11,2023&nbsp;/PRNewswire/ --&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;),
a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results
for the first&nbsp;quarterended&nbsp;March 31, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Mr. Zhenyong Liu, Chairman
and Chief Executive Officer of the Company, commented,&ldquo;In the first quarter of 2023, we had the revenue increased by 27.83% to&nbsp;approximately
$19.79million.As the Chinese government carried out a serious economic stimulus and support policies, this will definitely improve the
demand and overall operating environment for paper-making industry. We will seize the chance by taking management measures, such as optimizing
raw material procurement, diversifying the product structure and reducing cost to improve the profitability and prepare for the market
recovery.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>First Quarter 2023Unaudited
Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">For the first quarter
of 2023, total revenue increased by 27.83%, to&nbsp;approximately $19.79million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $15.48 million&nbsp;for the
same period of last year. This was mainly due to the increase in sales volume of corrugating medium paper (&ldquo;CMP&rdquo;), partially
offset by the decrease of average selling prices of CMP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">The following table summarizes
revenue, volume and ASP by product for the first quarter of 2023 and 2022, respectively:</P>

    <TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: right">32</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: right">57</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: right">1,160</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: right">49</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
  </TABLE>


<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, increased by 29.96%, to&nbsp;approximately $19.53 million&nbsp;and accounted for 98.67% of total revenue for the first
quarter of 2023, compared to&nbsp;approximately $15.03million, or 97.06% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 49,682tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$393/tonne in the first quarter of 2023, compared to 29,086&nbsp;tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$517/tonne
in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMPincreased
by25.72%, to&nbsp;approximately $16.47 million for the first quarter of 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $13.10million
for the same period of last year. The Company sold 41,663tonnesof regular CMPat an ASP of&nbsp;$395/tonne during the first quarter of
2023, compared to25,245tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$519/tonnefor the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMPincreased by
58.77%, to&nbsp;approximately $3.06 million for the first quarter of 2023, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $1.93 million for
the same period of last year. The Company sold8,019tonnesof light-weight CMPat an ASP of&nbsp;$382/tonne for the first quarter of 2023,
compared to3,841tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$502/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil &nbsp;for
the first quarter of 2023 and 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper
products decreased by 44.04%, to&nbsp;approximately $0.22million for the first quarter of 2023, from&nbsp;approximately&nbsp;$0.40 million&nbsp;for
the same period of last year. The Company sold 191tonnesof tissue paper products at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,167/tonne for the first quarter
of 2023, compared to 397tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$1,003/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from face masks
decreased by 37.03%, to&nbsp;approximately $35,637&nbsp;for the first quarter ended&nbsp;March 31, 2023, from $56,596for the same period
of last year. The Company sold 1,105 thousand pieces of face masks for the first quarter of2023, compared to1,160 thousand pieces of face
masks for the same period oflast year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit (Loss)
and Gross Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales increased by 32.30%, to&nbsp;approximately
$20.02million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2023 from&nbsp;approximately $15.13million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. The increase
in overall cost of saleswas mainly due to the increase in sales quantity of CMP, partially offset by the decrease in material costs of
CMP.&nbsp; Costs of sales per tonne for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, and tissue paper products were&nbsp;$388,&nbsp;$367,$nil
and&nbsp;$4,865, respectively, for the first quarter of 2023, compared to $491,&nbsp;$461,&nbsp;$nil&nbsp;and&nbsp;$2,424, respectively,
for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross losswas&nbsp;approximately $0.28million&nbsp;for
the first quarter of 2023, compared to the gross profit of&nbsp;approximately $0.31 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year as a
result of factors described above. Overall gross lossmargin was 1.40% for the first quarter of 2023, compared to gross profit margin was2.01%
for the same period of last year. Gross profit(loss)margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing paper, tissue paper products
and face mask products were 1.93%, 3.96%, nil%, -316.80% and -7.97%, respectively, for the first quarter of 2023, compared to 5.35%, 8.15%,
nil%, -141.51% and 29.47%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Selling, General and
Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Selling, general and
administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) decreased by 24.40%, to&nbsp;approximately $2.50million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2023
from&nbsp;approximately $3.30million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Loss from operations
was&nbsp;approximately $2.77 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2023, a decrease of 7.29%, from $2.99 million&nbsp;for the same
period of last year. Operating loss margin was 14.01% for the first quarter of 2023, compared to 19.32% for the same period of last
year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately
$2.73million, or loss per share of $0.27 for the first quarter of 2023, compared to $2.49 million, or loss per share of $0.25 for the
same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately
$1.21million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2023, compared to&nbsp;$1.20 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S.
GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange
Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA
is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to
investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation
of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures
of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>Cash, Liquidity and
Financial Position</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">As of&nbsp;March 31, 2023, the Company had cash
and bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term loans from credit union and related party loans),
and long-term debt (including related party loans) of&nbsp;approximately $16.75million,&nbsp;$11.67million and&nbsp;$6.51million, respectively,
comparedto &nbsp;approximately$9.52&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$11.16&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$4.20million, respectively, as of&nbsp;December 31,
2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net accounts receivable
was&nbsp;approximately $2.23&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;March 31, 2023, compared to approximately&nbsp;$nil&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;December
31, 2022. Net inventory was approximately&nbsp;$5.97&nbsp;million as of&nbsp;March 31, 2023, compared to&nbsp;approximately$2.87&nbsp;million
as of&nbsp;December 31, 2022. As of&nbsp;March 31, 2023, the Company had current assets of&nbsp;approximately$51.48&nbsp;million and current
liabilities of&nbsp;approximately$18.13 million, resulting in a working capital of&nbsp;approximately$33.35&nbsp;million. This was compared
to current assets of approximately $47.17 million and current liabilities of approximately $17.64 million, resulting in a working capital
of approximately $29.53 millionas of&nbsp;December 31, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Net cash provided by operating activities was&nbsp;approximately$4.81million&nbsp;for
the first quarter of 2023, compared to approximately&nbsp;$4.41 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. Net cash used in investing
activities was&nbsp;approximately$0.30 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2023, compared toapproximately$7.18 million&nbsp;for the
same period of last year. Net cash provided by financing activities was&nbsp;approximately$2.56million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2023,
compared to approximately$6.89 for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>About IT Tech Packaging,
Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Founded in 1996, IT Tech
Packaging, Inc. is a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North China.
Using recycled paper as its primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes three
categories of paper products: corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based in Baoding
and Xingtai in&nbsp;North China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region,
home to a growing base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the
country. ITP has been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;http://www.itpackaging.cn/.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
